                  <foreign lang="ar">هَمٌّ</foreign>: (K:) or [<foreign lang="ar">هَمٌّ</foreign>, accord. to common usage, is for some evil that is expected to happen; whereas] <foreign lang="ar">حُزْنٌ</foreign> is <hi rend="ital">grief arising on account of an unpleasant event that has happened,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">on account of an object of love that has passed away;</hi> and is the <hi rend="ital">contr. of</hi>

(TA.) [Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">عَامُ الحُزْنِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The year</hi> [<hi rend="ital">of mourning;</hi>] <hi rend="ital">in which died Khadeejeh and Aboo-Tálib:</hi> (IAar, Th, K:) so called by Mohammad.
